				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h1>Marketing Tom Blog</h1>
<h2>Our Latest News</h2>
<p>Did you know that Marketing Tom started life as a digital marketing blog? It then developed into a CIM Accredited Study Centre delivering both Accredited and Non-accredited courses. And, 16 years later, we are still blogging!</p></div>

			<article id="post-30309" class="et_pb_post clearfix et_pb_blog_item_0_0 post-30309 post type-post status-publish format-standard has-post-thumbnail hentry category-blogging category-email-marketing category-google category-google-adwordsadsense category-google-analytics category-internet category-marketing-tom-media category-new-technologies category-seo-world category-social-media category-twitter">

				<div class="et_pb_image_container"><a href="https://marketingtommedia.co.uk/exploiting-the-full-potential-of-chatbot-how-chatgpt-can-improve-your-digital-marketing-roi/" class="entry-featured-image-url"><img decoding="async" src="https://marketingtommedia.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/alex-knight-2EJCSULRwC8-unsplash-2-2-400x250.jpg" alt="Exploiting the full potential of chatbot: How ChatGPT can improve your digital marketing ROI" class="" srcset="https://marketingtommedia.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/alex-knight-2EJCSULRwC8-unsplash-2-2.jpg 479w, https://marketingtommedia.co.uk/wp-content/uploads/2023/01/alex-knight-2EJCSULRwC8-unsplash-2-2-400x250.jpg 480w " sizes="(max-width:479px) 479px, 100vw "  width="400" height="250" /></a></div>
														<h2 class="entry-title"><a href="https://marketingtommedia.co.uk/exploiting-the-full-potential-of-chatbot-how-chatgpt-can-improve-your-digital-marketing-roi/">Exploiting the full potential of chatbot: How ChatGPT can improve your digital marketing ROI</a></h2>
				
					<p class="post-meta"><span class="published">Jan 11, 2023</span></p><div class="post-content"><div class="post-content-inner"><p>Humans are the most adaptable creature on earth, not least according to humans! A big part of our adaptability rests on our ability to create tools for "doing more with less", which is a good definition of technology. (Forbes)So, you've probably all heard about...</p>
</div></div>
